####################################
#   v1.6.1.19 - (2018-05-28)
####################################

    Fixed bugs:

    BO: Fix directory listing

#   v1.6.1.18 - (2018-02-05)
####################################

    Fixed bugs:

    BO: Move to HTTPS
    BO: Update marketplace URL to http(S)
    BO: Fix AdminController's processDeleteImage() redirect after URL
    BO: Fix stock available after add product in order
    BO: Fix selecting a product does not work on Mac
    BO: Update AdminModulesController.php
    BO: Fix Stock cover report stock out calculation
    BO: Revert "Add paid order to stats dashboard even when there's no related invoice generated"

    FO: Hide the password in the confirmation email
    FO: Fix the blank page when no currency defined in the shop
    FO: Fix the sorting problem with a descending order in the products filtering page
    FO: Split width of summary invoice pdf
    FO: Fix conditionals check in DiscountController
    FO: Fix the email validator

    CO: Fixed for duplication of product which has both combinations and specific prices
    CO: Fix error 500, result of built-in function in write context
    CO: Fix PHP 7.1 compatibility
    CO: Increase limit message chars
    CO: Fix PHP Warning when updating category with multishop
    CO: Add DB prefix in delete() method all time $add_prefix is set to true
    CO: Clean the DB after language delete
    CO: Use english email template as fallback in getEmailTemplateContent

    IN: Update Postal Code of South Korea

    WS: Fix the update product web service
